pipeline for evaluating alert rules and dispatching notifications through the following components:\\n\\n## Rule Scheduler\\nThe core scheduler is implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`. The `schedule` struct manages a registry of alert rules and executes their evaluations on a configured interval via the `Run()` method. It uses `processTick()` to determine which rules should be evaluated in the current tick based on their evaluation interval.\\n\\n## Alert Rule Evaluation\\nIndividual alert rules are wrapped in the `alertRule` struct (`pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`), created by `newAlertRule()`. When scheduled, the rule's `Eval()` method queues an evaluation message. The `evaluate()` method executes the actual evaluation by:\\n1. Creating an evaluator using the evaluator factory\\n2. Executing the rule's condition queries against data sources\\n3. Calling the state manager's `ProcessEvalResults()` with the results\\n4. Sending state transitions via the callback to `send()`\\n\\n## Evaluation Engine\\nThe `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go` package contains the evaluation logic. The `conditionEvaluator` executes the rule's condition pipeline through the expression service, handling queries and expressions. The `EvaluateAlert()` function processes the query responses and determines the alert state for each instance. The `NewEvaluatorFactory()` creates evaluators configured with timeout and result limits.\\n\\n## Alert State Management\\nThe state manager (`pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`) maintains the `Manager` which processes evaluation results. The `ProcessEvalResults()` method:\\n1. Determines new states for each alert instance using the current rule definition\\n2. Handles state transitions (Alerting -> Normal, Error -> Alerting, etc.)\\n3. Records state changes to the historian\\n4. Invokes the sender callback with state transitions that need notification\\n\\nIndividual alert states are represented by the `State` struct (`pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go`). State transitions are computed by the `transition()` method, which applies rules for state changes (resultNormal, resultAlerting, resultError, resultNoData handlers) and determines when to resolve alerts.\\n\\n## Alert Routing and Dispatch\\nThe `AlertsRouter` (`pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`) routes evaluated alerts to appropriate destinations. Its `Send()` method determines whether to send alerts to:\\n1. The internal Alertmanager via `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()`, which calls `alertmanager.PutAlerts()`\\n2. External Alertmanager(s) via `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()`\\n\\nThe routing decision is based on the organization's alerting configuration and feature flags.\\n\\n## Internal Alertmanager\\nThe `MultiOrgAlertmanager` (`pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`) manages organization-specific alertmanagers. Each organization has an `alertmanager` instance (`pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go`) that wraps the `GrafanaAlertmanager` from the grafana/alerting library. The `PutAlerts()` method accepts postable alerts and passes them to the underlying alertmanager's routing and notification logic.\\n\\n## Notification Receivers\\nThe `ReceiverService` (`pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/receiver_svc.go`) manages the configuration and execution of notification receivers (email, webhook, etc.). Receivers are defined in the alertmanager configuration and receive alerts that match their routing rules.\\n\\n## Integration Point\\nThe main service initialization in `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go` wires all components together, creating the schedule, state manager, router, and multi-org alertmanager, and starting them in the service lifecycle.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":869,"cache_read_input_tokens":68725,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":869},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"8ecfb0da-7bc8-430a-8918-2534f47551dd","uuid":"fc2cd09c-144e-4dd4-8ac8-5220912d0692"}

pipeline for evaluating alert rules and dispatching notifications through the following components:\\n\\n## Rule Scheduler\\nThe core scheduler is implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`. The `schedule` struct manages a registry of alert rules and executes their evaluations on a configured interval via the `Run()` method. It uses `processTick()` to determine which rules should be evaluated in the current tick based on their evaluation interval.\\n\\n## Alert Rule Evaluation\\nIndividual alert rules are wrapped in the `alertRule` struct (`pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`), created by `newAlertRule()`. When scheduled, the rule's `Eval()` method queues an evaluation message. The `evaluate()` method executes the actual evaluation by:\\n1. Creating an evaluator using the evaluator factory\\n2. Executing the rule's condition queries against data sources\\n3. Calling the state manager's `ProcessEvalResults()` with the results\\n4. Sending state transitions via the callback to `send()`\\n\\n## Evaluation Engine\\nThe `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go` package contains the evaluation logic. The `conditionEvaluator` executes the rule's condition pipeline through the expression service, handling queries and expressions. The `EvaluateAlert()` function processes the query responses and determines the alert state for each instance. The `NewEvaluatorFactory()` creates evaluators configured with timeout and result limits.\\n\\n## Alert State Management\\nThe state manager (`pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`) maintains the `Manager` which processes evaluation results. The `ProcessEvalResults()` method:\\n1. Determines new states for each alert instance using the current rule definition\\n2. Handles state transitions (Alerting -> Normal, Error -> Alerting, etc.)\\n3. Records state changes to the historian\\n4. Invokes the sender callback with state transitions that need notification\\n\\nIndividual alert states are represented by the `State` struct (`pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go`). State transitions are computed by the `transition()` method, which applies rules for state changes (resultNormal, resultAlerting, resultError, resultNoData handlers) and determines when to resolve alerts.\\n\\n## Alert Routing and Dispatch\\nThe `AlertsRouter` (`pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`) routes evaluated alerts to appropriate destinations. Its `Send()` method determines whether to send alerts to:\\n1. The internal Alertmanager via `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()`, which calls `alertmanager.PutAlerts()`\\n2. External Alertmanager(s) via `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()`\\n\\nThe routing decision is based on the organization's alerting configuration and feature flags.\\n\\n## Internal Alertmanager\\nThe `MultiOrgAlertmanager` (`pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`) manages organization-specific alertmanagers. Each organization has an `alertmanager` instance (`pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go`) that wraps the `GrafanaAlertmanager` from the grafana/alerting library. The `PutAlerts()` method accepts postable alerts and passes them to the underlying alertmanager's routing and notification logic.\\n\\n## Notification Receivers\\nThe `ReceiverService` (`pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/receiver_svc.go`) manages the configuration and execution of notification receivers (email, webhook, etc.). Receivers are defined in the alertmanager configuration and receive alerts that match their routing rules.\\n\\n## Integration Point\\nThe main service initialization in `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go` wires all components together, creating the schedule, state manager, router, and multi-org alertmanager, and starting them in the service lifecycle.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
